italy_PPI_infighting ={ 
	if ={ 
		limit ={ 
			has_government = social_conservative
			has_idea = ITA_PPI_Factionalism_high_unity
		}
		set_variable = {
			variable = PPI_pp_debuff
			value = -0.05
		}
	}
	else_if ={ 
		limit ={ 
			has_government = social_conservative
			has_idea = ITA_PPI_Factionalism_medium_unity
		}
		set_variable = {
			variable = PPI_pp_debuff
			value = -0.15
		}
	}
	else_if ={ 
		limit ={ 
			has_government = social_conservative
			has_idea = ITA_PPI_Factionalism_low_unity
		}
		set_variable = {
			variable = PPI_pp_debuff
			value = -0.45
		}
	}
	else ={ 
		set_variable = {
			variable = PPI_pp_debuff
			value = 0
		}
	}
}
italy_setup_parliament ={ 

	clear_array = ITA_parliament_party_array
	clear_array = ITA_parliament_party_alignment_array

	set_variable = { ITA_parliament_size = 300}

	#party array

	add_to_array = { ITA_parliament_party_array = 1 }
	add_to_array = { ITA_parliament_party_array = 2 }
	add_to_array = { ITA_parliament_party_array = 3 }
	add_to_array = { ITA_parliament_party_array = 4 }
	add_to_array = { ITA_parliament_party_array = 5 }
	add_to_array = { ITA_parliament_party_array = 6 }
	add_to_array = { ITA_parliament_party_array = 7 }
	add_to_array = { ITA_parliament_party_array = 8 }
	add_to_array = { ITA_parliament_party_array = 9 }
	add_to_array = { ITA_parliament_party_array = 10 }
	add_to_array = { ITA_parliament_party_array = 11 }

	add_to_array = { ITA_parliament_party_alignment_array = 1 }
	add_to_array = { ITA_parliament_party_alignment_array = 2 }
	add_to_array = { ITA_parliament_party_alignment_array = 3 }
	add_to_array = { ITA_parliament_party_alignment_array = 4 }
	add_to_array = { ITA_parliament_party_alignment_array = 5 }
	add_to_array = { ITA_parliament_party_alignment_array = 6 }
	add_to_array = { ITA_parliament_party_alignment_array = 7 }
	add_to_array = { ITA_parliament_party_alignment_array = 8 }
	add_to_array = { ITA_parliament_party_alignment_array = 9 }
	add_to_array = { ITA_parliament_party_alignment_array = 10 }
	add_to_array = { ITA_parliament_party_alignment_array = 11 }

	#1 =MNI/Nationalists
	set_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_alignment_array^0 = 2 } #1 = coalition, 2 = abstain, 3 = opposition
	set_variable ={ ITA_parliament_party_array^0 = 4}
	# CDNL (Hardliners)
	set_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_alignment_array^1 = 2 }
	set_variable ={ ITA_parliament_party_array^1 = 10}
	# CDNL (Moderates)
	set_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_alignment_array^2 = 2 }
	set_variable ={ ITA_parliament_party_array^2 = 13}
	# PPI (right)
	set_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_alignment_array^3 = 1 }
	set_variable ={ ITA_parliament_party_array^3 = 42}
	# PPI (centre)
	set_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_alignment_array^4 = 1 }
	set_variable ={ ITA_parliament_party_array^4 = 62}
	# PPI (left)
	set_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_alignment_array^5 = 1 }
	set_variable ={ ITA_parliament_party_array^5 = 31}
	# PLI
	set_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_alignment_array^6 = 1 }
	set_variable ={ ITA_parliament_party_array^6 = 5}
	# PLD
	set_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_alignment_array^7 = 1 }
	set_variable ={ ITA_parliament_party_array^7 = 15}
	# PRI
	set_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_alignment_array^8 = 2 }
	set_variable ={ ITA_parliament_party_array^8 = 67}
	# PDL
	set_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_alignment_array^9 = 3 }
	set_variable ={ ITA_parliament_party_array^9 = 50}
	# NPS/socialists 
	set_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_alignment_array^10 = 3 }
	set_variable ={ ITA_parliament_party_array^10 = 1}

	ITA_calculate_alignment_size = yes
}

ITA_parliament_election_effect = {
	add_to_temp_array = { temp_popularity_array = party_popularity@national_populist }
	add_to_temp_array = { temp_popularity_array = party_popularity@paternal_autocrat }
	add_to_temp_array = { temp_popularity_array = party_popularity@authoritarian_democrat }
	set_temp_variable = { PPI_right_popularity = party_popularity@social_conservative} #PPI right
	multiply_temp_variable = { PPI_right_popularity = 0.25}
	add_to_temp_array = { temp_popularity_array = PPI_right_popularity}
	set_temp_variable = { PPI_centre_popularity = party_popularity@social_conservative} #PPI centre
	multiply_temp_variable = { PPI_centre_popularity = 0.5}
	add_to_temp_array = { temp_popularity_array = PPI_centre_popularity}
	set_temp_variable = { PPI_left_popularity = party_popularity@social_conservative} #PPI left
	multiply_temp_variable = { PPI_left_popularity = 0.25}
	add_to_temp_array = { temp_popularity_array = PPI_left_popularity}
	add_to_temp_array = { temp_popularity_array = party_popularity@market_liberal }
	add_to_temp_array = { temp_popularity_array = party_popularity@social_liberal }
	add_to_temp_array = { temp_popularity_array = party_popularity@revolutionary_republican }
	add_to_temp_array = { temp_popularity_array = party_popularity@social_democrat }
	add_to_temp_array = { temp_popularity_array = party_popularity@radical_socialist }


	for_each_loop = {
		array = temp_popularity_array

		multiply_temp_variable = { temp_popularity_array^i = ITA_parliament_size } # get number of seats for each party via multiplying popularity percent with total seats
		round_temp_variable = temp_popularity_array^i
		add_to_temp_variable = { temp_total = temp_popularity_array^i }
	}

	# sanity check to ensure total adds up to ITA_parliament_size
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { temp_total < ITA_parliament_size }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { temp_seat = ITA_parliament_size }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp_seat = temp_total }
		find_highest_in_array = { array = temp_popularity_array index = highest_index }
		add_to_temp_variable = { temp_popularity_array^highest_index = temp_seat }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { temp_total > ITA_parliament_size }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { temp_total = ITA_parliament_size }
		find_highest_in_array = { array = temp_popularity_array index = highest_index }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp_popularity_array^highest_index = temp_total }
	}

	# set seats for each party

	for_each_loop = {
		array = ITA_parliament_party_array

		set_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_array^i = temp_popularity_array^i }
	}
	ITA_calculate_alignment_size = yes
}
ITA_calculate_alignment_size ={ #basically calculate total coalition/opposition/abstention
	clear_variable = ITA_coalition_seats
	clear_variable = ITA_abstention_seats
	clear_variable = ITA_opposition_seats

	for_each_loop ={ 
		array = ITA_parliament_party_alignment_array

		if ={ 
			limit ={ 
				check_variable = {
					ITA_parliament_party_alignment_array^i = 1
				}
			}
			add_to_variable ={ 
				ITA_coalition_seats = ITA_parliament_party_array^i
			}
		}
		if ={ 
			limit ={ 
				check_variable = {
					ITA_parliament_party_alignment_array^i = 2
				}
			}
			add_to_variable ={ 
				ITA_abstention_seats = ITA_parliament_party_array^i
			}
		}
		if ={ 
			limit ={ 
				check_variable = {
					ITA_parliament_party_alignment_array^i = 3
				}
			}
			add_to_variable ={ 
				ITA_opposition_seats = ITA_parliament_party_array^i
			}
		}
	}
}


ITA_divided_whale_healing = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = ITA_ppi_internal_divisions_idea_3
		}
		remove_ideas = ITA_ppi_internal_divisions_idea_3
	}
	else = {
		effect_tooltip = {
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = ITA_ppi_internal_divisions_idea
				add_idea = ITA_ppi_internal_divisions_idea_2
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = ITA_ppi_internal_divisions_idea
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = ITA_ppi_internal_divisions_idea
					add_idea = ITA_ppi_internal_divisions_idea_2
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = ITA_ppi_internal_divisions_idea_2
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = ITA_ppi_internal_divisions_idea_2
					add_idea = ITA_ppi_internal_divisions_idea_3
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

ITA_1949_ppi_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_completed_focus = ITA_allow_catholic_action_expansion
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = 0.04
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = 0.06
		}
	}
	else = {
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = 0.04
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = 0.05
		}
	}
}
ITA_1949_ds_effect = {
	add_popularity = {
		ideology = market_liberal
		popularity = 0.05
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_completed_focus = ITA_absorb_federalist_organisations
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = -0.005
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = -0.005
		}
	}
}
ITA_clear_down_republicans = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = ITA_republicans_last_stand
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = ITA_republicans_last_stand
			add_idea = ITA_republicans_last_stand_2
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = ITA_republicans_last_stand_2
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = ITA_republicans_last_stand_2
			add_idea = ITA_republicans_last_stand_3
		}
	}
	else_if = { 
		limit = {
			has_idea = ITA_republicans_last_stand_3
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = ITA_republicans_last_stand_3
			add_idea = ITA_republicans_last_stand_4
		}
	}
	else_if = { 
		limit = {
			has_idea = ITA_republicans_last_stand_4
		}
		remove_ideas = ITA_republicans_last_stand_4
	}
	else = {
		add_political_power = 5
	}
}

ITA_1954_clear_gov_formation = {
	set_variable = { representatives_support_gov_formation = 0 }
	set_variable = { ita_1954_gov_formation_cost = 0 }
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = ITA_stable_government_formed_1954
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = deal_with_pe
		clr_country_flag = deal_with_pdc
		clr_country_flag = deal_with_dc
		clr_country_flag = deal_with_pli
		clr_country_flag = deal_with_pcdi
		clr_country_flag = deal_with_pda
	}
}
ITA_1954_create_government = {
	coal_rev_all = yes
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_government = social_democrat
					has_country_flag = deal_with_dc
				}
				AND = {
					has_government = social_conservative
					has_country_flag = deal_with_pda
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = KRG_ITA_1954_DC_PdA_government
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_government = social_liberal
					has_country_flag = deal_with_dc
				}
				AND = {
					has_government = social_conservative
					has_country_flag = deal_with_pcdi
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = KRG_ITA_1954_DC_PCdI_government
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_government = social_liberal
					has_country_flag = deal_with_pda
				}
				AND = {
					has_government = social_democrat
					has_country_flag = deal_with_pcdi
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = KRG_ITA_1954_PCdI_PdA_government
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = deal_with_pe
		}
		coal_add_pat_aut = yes
		clr_country_flag = deal_with_pe
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = deal_with_pdc
		}
		coal_add_auth_dem = yes
		clr_country_flag = deal_with_pdc
		activate_mission = KRG_ITA_1954_veterans_will_leave_government
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = deal_with_dc
		}
		coal_add_soc_con = yes
		clr_country_flag = deal_with_dc
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = social_conservative
				}
			}
			activate_mission = KRG_ITA_1954_dc_will_leave_government
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = deal_with_pli
		}
		coal_add_mar_lib = yes
		clr_country_flag = deal_with_pli
		activate_mission = KRG_ITA_1954_liberals_will_leave_government
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = deal_with_pcdi
		}
		coal_add_soc_lib = yes
		clr_country_flag = deal_with_pcdi
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = social_liberal
				}
			}
			activate_mission = KRG_ITA_1954_farmers_will_leave_government
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = deal_with_pda
		}
		coal_add_soc_dem = yes
		clr_country_flag = deal_with_pda
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = social_democrat
				}
			}
			activate_mission = KRG_ITA_1954_actionists_will_leave_government
		}
	}
	ITA_parliament_reload = yes
	mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
}
ITA_1954_socdem_increase_tensions = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = ITA_1954_socdem_large_split
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = ITA_1954_socdem_increase_tensions
	}
	add_political_power = 25
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = ITA_1954_socdem_medium_split
		}
		clr_country_flag = ITA_1954_socdem_medium_split
		set_country_flag = ITA_1954_socdem_large_split
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = ITA_1954_socdem_no_split
		}
		clr_country_flag = ITA_1954_socdem_no_split
	}
	else = {
		set_country_flag = ITA_1954_socdem_medium_split
	}
}
ITA_1954_socdem_decrease_tensions = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = ITA_1954_socdem_no_split
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = ITA_1954_socdem_decrease_tensions
	}
	add_political_power = -50
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = ITA_1954_socdem_large_split
		}
		clr_country_flag = ITA_1954_socdem_large_split
		set_country_flag = ITA_1954_socdem_medium_split
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = ITA_1954_socdem_medium_split
		}
		clr_country_flag = ITA_1954_socdem_medium_split
	}
	else = {
		set_country_flag = ITA_1954_socdem_no_split
	}
}

KRG_ITA_gov_king_bad = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = KRG_ITA_gov_king_bad
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = ITA_king_highly_supportive
		}
		clr_country_flag = ITA_king_highly_supportive
		set_country_flag = ITA_king_supportive
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = ITA_king_supportive
		}
		clr_country_flag = ITA_king_supportive
		set_country_flag = ITA_king_neutral
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = ITA_king_neutral
		}
		clr_country_flag = ITA_king_neutral
		set_country_flag = ITA_king_opposed
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = ITA_king_opposed
		}
		clr_country_flag = ITA_king_opposed
		set_country_flag = ITA_king_deeply_opposed
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = ITA_king_deeply_opposed
		}
		add_political_power = -25
	}
	ITA_parliament_reload = yes
}

ITA_montreal_wk3_effect = {
	news_event = {
		id = krg_ita_dnf.15
		days = 5
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = villa_giusti_summit_ongoing
		}
		country_event = krg_ita_dnf.12 # Villa Giusti Summit cancelled
		DNF = {
			country_event = krg_ita_dnf.12 # Villa Giusti Summit cancelled
		}
	}
	else = {
		DNF = {
			country_event = krg_ita_dnf.13 # Italy renounces Montreal
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = robert_affair_ongoing
		}
		country_event = krg_ita_dnf.14 # A New Radious May
	}
}

ITA_crisis_escalation_effect = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = ITA_crisis_escalation_inc_tt
	add_to_variable = { ITA.crisis_escalation_level = 1 }
	hidden_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { ITA.crisis_escalation_level = 1 }
			}
			ITA = {
				country_event = krg_ita.159
			}
			ITA = {
				country_event = krg_ita.159
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { ITA.crisis_escalation_level = 2 }
			#	DNF = {
				#	NOT = {
				#		has_completed_focus = DNF_stay_out
				#	}
			#	}
			}
			ITA = {
				country_event = krg_ita.168
			}
			ITA = {
				country_event = krg_ita.168
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { ITA.crisis_escalation_level = 3 }
			}
			DNF = {
				country_event = krg_ita.171
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { ITA.crisis_escalation_level = 5 }
			}
			ENT = {
				remove_from_faction = ITA
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					DNF = {
						has_guaranteed = ITA
					}
				}
				DNF = {
					diplomatic_relation = {
						country = ITA
						relation = guarantee
						active = no
					}
				}
				set_global_flag = dnf_guarantee_italy_inactive
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					ITA = {
						owns_state = 2
					}
				}
				ITA = {
					declare_war_on = {
						target = ITA
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				ITA = {
					declare_war_on = {
						target = ITA
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = dnf_guarantee_italy_inactive
				}
				DNF = {
					give_guarantee = ITA
				}
				clr_global_flag = dnf_guarantee_italy_inactive
			}
			ITA = {
				country_event = {
					id = krg_ita.174
					days = 15
				}
				country_event = {
					id = krg_ita.175
					days = 15
				}
			}
			news_event = krg_ita.176
		}
	}
}

ITA_crisis_deescalation_effect = { # deescalation isn't possible atm
	custom_effect_tooltip = ITA_crisis_deescalation_inc_tt
	subtract_from_variable = {  ITA.crisis_escalation_level = 1 }
}

	clr_country_flag = prepared_southern_defence
	clr_country_flag = prepared_northern_defence
	clr_country_flag = lured_forces_south
	clr_country_flag = lured_forces_north
	clr_country_flag = prepared_southern_offensive
	clr_country_flag = prepared_northern_offensive

	clr_country_flag = prepared_northern_fake_intel
	clr_global_flag = roman_crisis_lured_forces_north
	clr_global_flag = roman_crisis_lured_forces_south
	clr_global_flag = roman_crisis_lured_defence_north
	clr_global_flag = roman_crisis_lured_defence_south
	clr_global_flag = roman_crisis_defence_victory
	clr_global_flag = roman_crisis_attack_victory

	set_variable = { ITA.roman_crisis_southern_defence = 0 }
	set_variable = { ITA.roman_crisis_northern_offensive = 0 }
	set_variable = { ITA.roman_crisis_southern_offensive = 0 }
}

ITA_parliament_initial = {
	clear_array = ITA_parliament_party_array

	# Party IDs
	set_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_FDP = 1 }
	set_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_PdA = 2 }
	set_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_PRI = 3 }
	set_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_DS = 4 }
	set_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_PPI = 5 }
	set_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_PLI = 6 }
	set_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_CNDL = 7 }
	set_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_UQ = 8 }

	# add parties
	add_to_array = { ITA_parliament_party_array = 1 } # FDP
	add_to_array = { ITA_parliament_party_array = 2 } # PdA
	add_to_array = { ITA_parliament_party_array = 3 } # PRI
	add_to_array = { ITA_parliament_party_array = 4 } # DS
	add_to_array = { ITA_parliament_party_array = 5 } # PPI
	add_to_array = { ITA_parliament_party_array = 6 } # PLI
	add_to_array = { ITA_parliament_party_array = 7 } # CNDL
	add_to_array = { ITA_parliament_party_array = 8 } # UQ

	clear_array = ITA_parliament_screen_array
	add_to_array = { ITA_parliament_screen_array = 1 }

	# calculate seats
	ITA_chamber_of_deputies_seat_reload = yes
	# not available at start yet
	#ITA_senate_seat_reload = yes
}

# for testing
ITA_parliament_initial_with_senate = {
	clear_array = ITA_parliament_party_array

	# add parties
	add_to_array = { ITA_parliament_party_array = 1 } # FDP
	add_to_array = { ITA_parliament_party_array = 2 } # PdA
	add_to_array = { ITA_parliament_party_array = 3 } # PRI
	add_to_array = { ITA_parliament_party_array = 4 } # DS
	add_to_array = { ITA_parliament_party_array = 5 } # PPI
	add_to_array = { ITA_parliament_party_array = 6 } # PLI
	add_to_array = { ITA_parliament_party_array = 7 } # CNDL
	add_to_array = { ITA_parliament_party_array = 8 } # UQ

	clear_array = ITA_parliament_screen_array
	add_to_array = { ITA_parliament_screen_array = 1 }

	set_country_flag = ITA_senate_reformed

	# calculate seats
	ITA_chamber_of_deputies_seat_reload = yes
	ITA_senate_seat_reload = yes
}

	custom_effect_tooltip = ITA_parliament_modify_alignment_tt

	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = ITA_senate_reformed }
		ITA_senate_reload = yes
	}
}

	custom_effect_tooltip = ITA_parliament_modify_support_tt

		limit = { has_country_flag = ITA_senate_reformed }

######################################################
# Usage:
# set_temp_variable = { temp_party_1 = <PARTY_ID> }
# set_temp_variable = { temp_party_2 = <PARTY_ID> }
# set_temp_variable = { temp_seat = <VALUE> }
# ITA_chamber_of_deputies_transfer_seat = yes
######################################################
# Transfer seat from party 1 to party 2
######################################################
ITA_chamber_of_deputies_transfer_seat = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = ITA_chamber_of_deputies_transfer_seat_tt

	set_temp_variable = { temp_total = temp_party_1:ITA_chamber_of_deputies_seat }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp_total = temp_seat }

	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { temp_total < 0 }
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = { temp_seat = temp_total }
	}

	add_to_variable = { temp_party_2:ITA_chamber_of_deputies_seat = temp_seat }
	subtract_from_variable = { temp_party_1:ITA_chamber_of_deputies_seat = temp_seat }

	ITA_chamber_of_deputies_reload = yes
}

######################################################
# Usage:
# set_temp_variable = { temp_party_1 = <PARTY_ID> }
# set_temp_variable = { temp_party_2 = <PARTY_ID> }
# set_temp_variable = { temp_seat = <VALUE> }
# ITA_senate_transfer_seat = yes
######################################################
# Transfer seat from party 1 to party 2
######################################################
ITA_senate_transfer_seat = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = ITA_senate_transfer_seat_tt

	set_temp_variable = { temp_total = temp_party_1:ITA_senate_seat }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp_total = temp_seat }

	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { temp_total < 0 }
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = { temp_seat = temp_total }
	}

	add_to_variable = { temp_party_2:ITA_senate_seat = temp_seat }
	subtract_from_variable = { temp_party_1:ITA_senate_seat = temp_seat }

	ITA_senate_reload = yes
}

##############################################

ITA_parliament_seat_reload = {
	ITA_chamber_of_deputies_seat_reload = yes

		ITA_senate_seat_reload = yes
	}
}

##################################################################
# Usage:
# ITA_chamber_of_deputies_seat_reload = yes
##################################################################
# Calculate new chamber of deputies seat values after elections
##################################################################
ITA_chamber_of_deputies_seat_reload = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = ITA_electoral_reform_next_elections
			NOT = { has_country_flag = ITA_dont_change_seat_numbers_yet }
		}
		# majority set at 268 / 535
		set_variable = { ITA_chamber_of_deputies_majority = 268 }

		# setup positions
		ITA_chamber_of_deputies_position_535 = yes
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ITA_chamber_of_deputies_x_array

			add_to_variable = { ITA_chamber_of_deputies_x_array^i = -47 }
		}
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ITA_chamber_of_deputies_y_array

			add_to_variable = { ITA_chamber_of_deputies_y_array^i = -25 }
		}
	}
	else = {
		# majority set at 255 / 508
		set_variable = { ITA_chamber_of_deputies_majority = 255 }

		# setup positions
		ITA_chamber_of_deputies_position_508 = yes
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ITA_chamber_of_deputies_x_array

			add_to_variable = { ITA_chamber_of_deputies_x_array^i = -32 }
		}
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ITA_chamber_of_deputies_y_array

			add_to_variable = { ITA_chamber_of_deputies_y_array^i = -20 }
		}
	}

	clear_array = temp_popularity_array

	add_to_temp_array = { temp_popularity_array = party_popularity@authoritarian_socialist } # FDP
	add_to_temp_array = { temp_popularity_array = party_popularity@social_democrat } # PdA

	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = ITA_agrarian_action_joined_pda }
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = { temp_popularity_array^0 = party_popularity@radical_socialist } # FDP
	}
	else = {
		add_to_temp_variable = { temp_popularity_array^1 = party_popularity@radical_socialist } # PdA
	}

	add_to_temp_array = { temp_popularity_array = party_popularity@revolutionary_republican } # PRI
	add_to_temp_array = { temp_popularity_array = party_popularity@market_liberal } # DS

	add_to_temp_array = { temp_popularity_array = party_popularity@social_conservative } # PPI
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp_popularity_array^4 = party_popularity@social_liberal } # PPI

	add_to_temp_array = { temp_popularity_array = party_popularity@authoritarian_democrat } # PLI
	add_to_temp_array = { temp_popularity_array = party_popularity@paternal_autocrat } # CNDL
	add_to_temp_array = { temp_popularity_array = party_popularity@national_populist } # UQ

	# calculate seats based on seat total and popularity
	for_each_loop = {
		array = temp_popularity_array

		multiply_temp_variable = { temp_popularity_array^i = ITA_chamber_of_deputies_x_array^num }
		round_temp_variable = temp_popularity_array^i
		add_to_temp_variable = { temp_total = temp_popularity_array^i }
	}

	# sanity check to ensure total adds up to seat total
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { temp_total < ITA_chamber_of_deputies_x_array^num }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { temp_seat = ITA_chamber_of_deputies_x_array^num }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp_seat = temp_total }
		find_highest_in_array = { array = temp_popularity_array index = highest_index }
		add_to_temp_variable = { temp_popularity_array^highest_index = temp_seat }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { temp_total > ITA_chamber_of_deputies_x_array^num }
		}
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp_total = ITA_chamber_of_deputies_x_array^num }
		find_highest_in_array = { array = temp_popularity_array index = highest_index }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp_popularity_array^highest_index = temp_total }
	}

	# set seats for each party
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ITA_parliament_party_array

		set_variable = { v:ITA_chamber_of_deputies_seat = temp_popularity_array^i }
	}

	ITA_chamber_of_deputies_reload = yes
}

#####################################################
# Usage:
# ITA_senate_seat_reload = yes
#####################################################
# Calculate new senate seat values after elections
#####################################################
ITA_senate_seat_reload = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = ITA_electoral_reform_next_elections
			NOT = { has_country_flag = ITA_dont_change_seat_numbers_yet }
		}
		# majority set at 135 / 268
		set_variable = { ITA_senate_majority = 268 }

		# setup positions
		ITA_senate_position_268 = yes
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ITA_senate_x_array

			add_to_variable = { ITA_senate_x_array^i = 0 }
		}
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ITA_senate_y_array

			add_to_variable = { ITA_senate_y_array^i = 0 }
		}
	}
	else = {
		# majority set at 128 / 254
		set_variable = { ITA_senate_majority = 255 }

		# setup positions
		ITA_senate_position_254 = yes
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ITA_senate_x_array

			add_to_variable = { ITA_senate_x_array^i = 0 }
		}
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ITA_senate_y_array

			add_to_variable = { ITA_senate_y_array^i = 0 }
		}
	}

	add_to_temp_array = { temp_popularity_2_array = party_popularity@authoritarian_socialist } # FDP
	add_to_temp_array = { temp_popularity_2_array = party_popularity@social_democrat } # PdA

	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = ITA_agrarian_action_joined_pda }
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = { temp_popularity_2_array^0 = party_popularity@radical_socialist } # FDP
	}
	else = {
		add_to_temp_variable = { temp_popularity_2_array^1 = party_popularity@radical_socialist } # PdA
	}

	add_to_temp_array = { temp_popularity_2_array = party_popularity@revolutionary_republican } # PRI
	add_to_temp_array = { temp_popularity_2_array = party_popularity@market_liberal } # DS

	add_to_temp_array = { temp_popularity_2_array = party_popularity@social_conservative } # PPI
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp_popularity_2_array^4 = party_popularity@social_liberal } # PPI

	add_to_temp_array = { temp_popularity_2_array = party_popularity@authoritarian_democrat } # PLI
	add_to_temp_array = { temp_popularity_2_array = party_popularity@paternal_autocrat } # CNDL
	add_to_temp_array = { temp_popularity_2_array = party_popularity@national_populist } # UQ

	# calculate seats based on seat total and popularity
	for_each_loop = {
		array = temp_popularity_2_array

		multiply_temp_variable = { temp_popularity_2_array^i = ITA_senate_x_array^num }
		round_temp_variable = temp_popularity_2_array^i
		add_to_temp_variable = { temp_total_2 = temp_popularity_2_array^i }
	}

	log = "[?temp_total_2]"

	# sanity check to ensure total adds up to seat total
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { temp_total_2 < ITA_senate_x_array^num }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { temp_seat = ITA_senate_x_array^num }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp_seat = temp_total_2 }
		find_highest_in_array = { array = temp_popularity_2_array index = highest_index }
		add_to_temp_variable = { temp_popularity_2_array^highest_index = temp_seat }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { temp_total_2 > ITA_senate_x_array^num }
		}
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp_total_2 = ITA_senate_x_array^num }
		find_highest_in_array = { array = temp_popularity_2_array index = highest_index }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp_popularity_2_array^highest_index = temp_total_2 }
	}

	# set seats for each party
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ITA_parliament_party_array

		set_variable = { v:ITA_senate_seat = temp_popularity_2_array^i }
	}

	ITA_senate_reload = yes
}

########################################
# Usage:
# ITA_parliament_reload = yes
########################################
# Reload Parliament GUI with new values
########################################
ITA_parliament_reload = {
	ITA_chamber_of_deputies_reload = yes
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = ITA_senate_reformed }
		ITA_senate_reload = yes
	}
}

################################################
# Usage:
# ITA_chamber_of_deputies_reload = yes
################################################
# Reload chamber of deputies with new values
################################################
ITA_chamber_of_deputies_reload = {
	clear_array = ITA_chamber_of_deputies_main_array
	clear_array = ITA_chamber_of_deputies_cosmetic_party_array
	clear_array = ITA_chamber_of_deputies_government_array
	clear_array = ITA_chamber_of_deputies_opposition_array
	clear_variable = ITA_chamber_of_deputies_government_seat
	clear_variable = ITA_chamber_of_deputies_opposition_seat
	clear_variable = ITA_chamber_of_deputies_support_total

	# set party alignment
	# FDP
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_government = authoritarian_socialist
				is_in_array = { coal_list = 1 }
				AND = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = ITA_agrarian_action_joined_pda }
					OR = {
						has_government = radical_socialist
						is_in_array = { coal_list = 2 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_FDP:ITA_parliament_alignment = 1 }
		set_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_FDP:ITA_parliament_support = 1 }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_FDP:ITA_parliament_alignment = 2 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					check_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_FDP:ITA_parliament_support = 2 }
				}
			}
			set_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_FDP:ITA_parliament_support = 3 }
		}
	}
	# PdA
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_government = social_democrat
				is_in_array = { coal_list = 3 }
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = ITA_agrarian_action_joined_pda
					OR = {
						has_government = radical_socialist
						is_in_array = { coal_list = 2 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_PdA:ITA_parliament_alignment = 1 }
		set_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_PdA:ITA_parliament_support = 1 }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_PdA:ITA_parliament_alignment = 2 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					check_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_PdA:ITA_parliament_support = 2 }
				}
			}
			set_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_PdA:ITA_parliament_support = 3 }
		}
	}
	# PRI
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_government = revolutionary_republican
				is_in_array = { coal_list = 4 }
			}
		}
		set_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_PRI:ITA_parliament_alignment = 1 }
		set_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_PRI:ITA_parliament_support = 1 }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_PRI:ITA_parliament_alignment = 2 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					check_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_PRI:ITA_parliament_support = 2 }
				}
			}
			set_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_PRI:ITA_parliament_support = 3 }
		}
	}
	# DS
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_government = market_liberal
				is_in_array = { coal_list = 6 }
			}
		}
		set_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_DS:ITA_parliament_alignment = 1 }
		set_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_DS:ITA_parliament_support = 1 }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_DS:ITA_parliament_alignment = 2 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					check_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_DS:ITA_parliament_support = 2 }
				}
			}
			set_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_DS:ITA_parliament_support = 3 }
		}
	}
	# PPI
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_government = social_conservative
				is_in_array = { coal_list = 7 }
				has_government = social_liberal
				is_in_array = { coal_list = 5 }
			}
		}
		set_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_PPI:ITA_parliament_alignment = 1 }
		set_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_PPI:ITA_parliament_support = 1 }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_PPI:ITA_parliament_alignment = 2 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					check_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_PPI:ITA_parliament_support = 2 }
				}
			}
			set_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_PPI:ITA_parliament_support = 3 }
		}
	}
	# PLI
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_government = authoritarian_democrat
				is_in_array = { coal_list = 8 }
			}
		}
		set_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_PLI:ITA_parliament_alignment = 1 }
		set_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_PLI:ITA_parliament_support = 1 }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_PLI:ITA_parliament_alignment = 2 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					check_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_PLI:ITA_parliament_support = 2 }
				}
			}
			set_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_PLI:ITA_parliament_support = 3 }
		}
	}
	# CNDL
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_government = paternal_autocrat
				is_in_array = { coal_list = 9 }
			}
		}
		set_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_CNDL:ITA_parliament_alignment = 1 }
		set_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_CNDL:ITA_parliament_support = 1 }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_CNDL:ITA_parliament_alignment = 2 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					check_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_CNDL:ITA_parliament_support = 2 }
				}
			}
			set_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_CNDL:ITA_parliament_support = 3 }
		}
	}
	# UQ
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_government = national_populist
				is_in_array = { coal_list = 10 }
			}
		}
		set_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_UQ:ITA_parliament_alignment = 1 }
		set_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_UQ:ITA_parliament_support = 1 }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_UQ:ITA_parliament_alignment = 2 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					check_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_UQ:ITA_parliament_support = 2 }
				}
			}
			set_variable = { ITA_parliament_party_UQ:ITA_parliament_support = 3 }
		}
	}

	# cut parties with no seats
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ITA_parliament_party_array

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { v:ITA_chamber_of_deputies_seat > 0 }
			}
			add_to_array = { ITA_chamber_of_deputies_cosmetic_party_array = v }
		}
	}

	# add party to respective alignment arrays
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ITA_chamber_of_deputies_cosmetic_party_array

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { v:ITA_parliament_alignment = 1 }
			}
			add_to_array = { ITA_chamber_of_deputies_government_array = v }
			add_to_variable = { ITA_chamber_of_deputies_government_seat = v:ITA_chamber_of_deputies_seat }
		}
		else = {
			add_to_array = { ITA_chamber_of_deputies_opposition_array = v }
			add_to_variable = { ITA_chamber_of_deputies_opposition_seat = v:ITA_chamber_of_deputies_seat }
		}
	}

	clear_array = ITA_chamber_of_deputies_cosmetic_party_array

	for_each_loop = {
		array = ITA_chamber_of_deputies_government_array

		add_to_array = { ITA_chamber_of_deputies_cosmetic_party_array = v }
	}

	for_each_loop = {
		array = ITA_chamber_of_deputies_opposition_array

		add_to_array = { ITA_chamber_of_deputies_cosmetic_party_array = v }
	}

	# add to main array each party seats
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ITA_chamber_of_deputies_cosmetic_party_array
		value = v1

		for_loop_effect = {
			start = 1
			end = v1:ITA_chamber_of_deputies_seat
			compare = less_than_or_equals

			add_to_array = { ITA_chamber_of_deputies_main_array = v1 }
		}
	}

	# calculate total support
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ITA_chamber_of_deputies_cosmetic_party_array

		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { v:ITA_parliament_support = 1 }
					check_variable = { v:ITA_parliament_support = 2 }
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { ITA_chamber_of_deputies_support_total = v:ITA_chamber_of_deputies_seat }
		}
	}

	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = ITA_electoral_reform_next_elections }
		ITA_chamber_of_deputies_position_535 = yes
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ITA_chamber_of_deputies_x_array

			add_to_variable = { ITA_chamber_of_deputies_x_array^i = -47 }
		}
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ITA_chamber_of_deputies_y_array

			add_to_variable = { ITA_chamber_of_deputies_y_array^i = -25 }
		}
	}
	else = {
		ITA_chamber_of_deputies_position_508 = yes
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ITA_chamber_of_deputies_x_array

			add_to_variable = { ITA_chamber_of_deputies_x_array^i = -32 }
		}
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ITA_chamber_of_deputies_y_array

			add_to_variable = { ITA_chamber_of_deputies_y_array^i = -20 }
		}
	}

	set_temp_variable = { temp_total = 0 }

	for_each_loop = {
		array = ITA_chamber_of_deputies_x_array

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { temp_total < ITA_chamber_of_deputies_government_seat }
			}
			add_to_temp_variable = { temp_total = 1 }
			add_to_variable = { ITA_chamber_of_deputies_x_array^i = -5 }
		}
		else = {
			add_to_variable = { ITA_chamber_of_deputies_x_array^i = 5 }
		}
	}

	add_to_variable = { ITA_parliament_dirty = 1 }
}

########################################
# Usage:
# ITA_senate_reload = yes
########################################
# Reload senate with new values
########################################
ITA_senate_reload = {
	clear_array = ITA_senate_main_array
	clear_array = ITA_senate_cosmetic_party_array
	clear_array = ITA_senate_government_array
	clear_array = ITA_senate_opposition_array
	clear_variable = ITA_senate_government_seat
	clear_variable = ITA_senate_opposition_seat
	clear_variable = ITA_senate_support_total

	# alignment already set in deputies effect

	# cut parties with no seats
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ITA_parliament_party_array

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { v:ITA_senate_seat > 0 }
			}
			add_to_array = { ITA_senate_cosmetic_party_array = v }
		}
	}

	# add party to respective alignment arrays
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ITA_senate_cosmetic_party_array

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { v:ITA_parliament_alignment = 1 }
			}
			add_to_array = { ITA_senate_government_array = v }
			add_to_variable = { ITA_senate_government_seat = v:ITA_senate_seat }
		}
		else = {
			add_to_array = { ITA_senate_opposition_array = v }
			add_to_variable = { ITA_senate_opposition_seat = v:ITA_senate_seat }
		}
	}

	clear_array = ITA_senate_cosmetic_party_array

	for_each_loop = {
		array = ITA_senate_government_array

		add_to_array = { ITA_senate_cosmetic_party_array = v }
	}

	for_each_loop = {
		array = ITA_senate_opposition_array

		add_to_array = { ITA_senate_cosmetic_party_array = v }
	}

	# add to main array each party seats
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ITA_senate_cosmetic_party_array
		value = v1

		for_loop_effect = {
			start = 1
			end = v1:ITA_senate_seat
			compare = less_than_or_equals

			add_to_array = { ITA_senate_main_array = v1 }
		}
	}

	# calculate total support
	for_each_loop = {
		array = ITA_senate_cosmetic_party_array

		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { v:ITA_parliament_support = 1 }
					check_variable = { v:ITA_parliament_support = 2 }
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { ITA_senate_support_total = v:ITA_senate_seat }
		}
	}

	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = ITA_electoral_reform_next_elections }
		ITA_senate_position_268 = yes
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ITA_senate_x_array

			add_to_variable = { ITA_senate_x_array^i = -47 }
		}
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ITA_senate_y_array

			add_to_variable = { ITA_senate_y_array^i = -25 }
		}
	}
	else = {
		ITA_senate_position_254 = yes
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ITA_senate_x_array

			add_to_variable = { ITA_senate_x_array^i = -32 }
		}
		for_each_loop = {
			array = ITA_senate_y_array

			add_to_variable = { ITA_senate_y_array^i = -20 }
		}
	}

	set_temp_variable = { temp_total = 0 }

	for_each_loop = {
		array = ITA_senate_x_array

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { temp_total < ITA_senate_government_seat }
			}
			add_to_temp_variable = { temp_total = 1 }
			add_to_variable = { ITA_senate_x_array^i = -5 }
		}
		else = {
			add_to_variable = { ITA_senate_x_array^i = 5 }
		}
	}

	add_to_variable = { ITA_parliament_dirty = 1 }
}
